            advertising: {
                client: "googima",
                admessage: 'Publicidade xx segundos',
                skiptext: "Pular",
                skipoffset: 5,
                companiondiv: { id: "pub-retangulo-player", width: 300, height: 250 }
            }
        }),
        createButton: (icon, label, action, id) => ([
            `https://s3.glbimg.com/v1/AUTH_3ec28e89a5754c7b937cbc7ade6b1ace/assets/player/${icon}`,
            label, action, id
        ]),
        previousAudio: () => {
            const index = player.instance.getPlaylistIndex();
            index > 0 ? player.instance.playlistItem(index - 1) : player.instance.seek(0);
        },
        rewind10s: () => player.instance.seek(player.instance.getPosition() - 10),
        forward10s: () => player.instance.seek(player.instance.getPosition() + 10),
        nextAudio: () => {
            const index = player.instance.getPlaylistIndex();
            index < player.instance.getPlaylist().length - 1 ? player.instance.playlistItem(index + 1) : player.instance.seek(0);
        },
        logEvent: (message, bgcolor = "#999") => console.log(`%c Player Event: ${message} `, `background-color: ${bgcolor}; color: white; font-weight: bold; border-radius: 10px;`),
        pushAnalytics: (event, action, label) => {
            try {
                console.log(`Analytics: push - ${event} - ${label}`);
                dataLayer.push({
                    event,
                    event_category: 'ao vivo',
                    ...(action && { event_action: action }),
                    event_label: encodeURI(label)
                });
            } catch {
                console.error(`Analytics Error: ${event}`);
            }
        },
        handleBeforePlay: () => {
            player.logEvent("Before Play");
            const item = player.instance.getPlaylistItem();
            const params = player.buildAdParams(item);
            const vast_url = player.buildVastUrl(params);
            try {
                player.instance.playAd(vast_url);
            } catch {
                player.instance.loadAdTag(vast_url);
            }
        },
        buildAdParams: (item) => ({
            adunit: `${ad_account_id}`,
            sz: "1280x720|640x480",
            cust_params: `${ad_custom_data}%26sgr_key%3Daovivo%2C${item.slug}%2C${encodeURI(item.show)}`,
            ciu_szs: "1x1,300x250",
            url: encodeURIComponent(location.href),
            description_url: encodeURIComponent(document.title),
            correlator: Date.now(),
            editoria_path: `/${hierarchy_path.toLowerCase().trim().replace(/\s*\/\s*/g, '/').replace(/\s+/g, '-') || ''}`
        }),
        buildVastUrl: (params) =>
            `https://pubads.g.doubleclick.net/gampad/ads?sz=${params.sz}&iu=/${params.adunit}${params.editoria_path}&cust_params=${params.cust_params}&ciu_szs=${params.ciu_szs}&impl=s&gdfp_req=1&env=vp&output=vmap&unviewed_position_start=1&url=${params.url}&description_url=${params.url}&correlator=${params.correlator}&hl=pt&vpmute=1&wta=0&vpos=preroll`,
        handleFirstFrame: () => {
            player.logEvent("First Frame");
            const item = player.instance.getPlaylistItem();
            player.pushAnalytics("start", "start", `${item.show} - ${item.slug}`);
        },
        handlePlay: () => {
            player.logEvent("Play", "#090");
            const item = player.instance.getPlaylistItem();
            if (!player.first_play) player.pushAnalytics("start", "play", `${item.show} - ${item.slug}`);
            player.last_audio_played = item.file;
            player.first_play = false;
        },
        handlePlayAttemptFailed: () => {
            player.logEvent("Play Attempt Failed", "#F00");
            const item = player.instance.getPlaylistItem();
            player.pushAnalytics("Play Attempt Failed", "Play Attempt Failed", `${item.show} - ${item.slug}`);
        },
        handlePause: () => {
            player.logEvent("Pause", "#060");
            const item = player.instance.getPlaylistItem();
            player.pushAnalytics("pause", "pause", `${item.show} - ${item.slug}`);
        },
        handleTime: ({ currentTime }) => {
            if (player.last_time_listened > 0 && player.last_time_listened % 30 === 0 && player.last_time_listened !== parseInt(currentTime)) {
                const item = player.instance.getPlaylistItem();
                player.pushAnalytics("refresh", undefined, `${item.show} - ${item.slug}`);
            }
            player.last_time_listened = parseInt(currentTime);
        }
    };

  const el = document.querySelector(".soccer-fixtures");
  const isCompact = el.dataset.compact === "true";
  el.dataset.compact = !isCompact;
}

  const targetElement = document.querySelector(targetId);
  if (targetElement) {
    window.scrollTo({
      top: targetElement.offsetTop - 70,
      behavior: 'smooth'
    });
  }
}

    const today = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];
    let foundIndex = -1;
    let lastIndex = -1;


    const parseDateFromString = (string) => {
      const parts = string.split('/');
      const dateWithoutTime = new Date(parts[2], parts[1] - 1, parts[0]);
      return dateWithoutTime.toISOString().split('T')[0];
    }

    const handleDateChange = function() {
      const el = document.querySelector(".agenda-futebol .card_header .date");
      const newDate = document.querySelector(".soccer-fixtures .swiper-slide-active .swiper-content").dataset.date;
      el.innerHTML = newDate;
    }
    
    
    jsdata.groupedArray.forEach((group, index) => {
      if (foundIndex == -1 && parseDateFromString(group.data_inicio) >= today) {
        console.log("data: " + parseDateFromString(group.data_inicio));
        console.log("Today: " + today);

        return foundIndex = index;
      }
      lastIndex = index;
    });
      
    if (foundIndex == -1) {
      foundIndex = lastIndex;
    }

    swiper.init();

  function base64UrlDecode(str) {
    let base64 = str.replace(/-/g, "+").replace(/_/g, "/");
    while (base64.length % 4) {
      base64 += "=";
    }
    return atob(base64);
  }

  function getCookie(cookieName) {
    var cookies = document.cookie.split(";");
    for (var i = 0; i < cookies.length; i++) {
      var cookie = cookies[i].trim();
      if (cookie.indexOf(cookieName + "=") === 0) {
        return cookie.substring(cookieName.length + 1);
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  function sendExternalId() {
    var cookie = getCookie("GLOBO_ID");
    if (cookie) {
      try {
        var payload = cookie.split(".")[1];
        var decoded = base64UrlDecode(payload);
        var user = JSON.parse(decoded);

      }
    } else {
      console.log("[ONESIGNAL] Error: GLOBO_ID cookie not found.");
    }
  }
